  def test_index


    		
  

  

  

    
      58

      59
    
    
      
      get :index


    		
  

  

  

    
      60
    
    
      
      assert_response :success


    		
  

  

  

    
      61
    
    
      
      assert_template 'index'


    		
  

  

  

    
      62
    
    
      
      assert_not_nil assigns(:issues)


    		
  

  

  

    
      63
    
    
      
      assert_nil assigns(:project)


    		
  

  

  

    
      64
    
    
      
      assert_tag :tag => 'a', :content => /Can't print recipes/


    		
  

  

  

    
      65

      66
    
    
      
      # private projects hidden


    		
  

  

  

    
      67
    
    
      
      assert_no_tag :tag => 'a', :content => /Issue of a private subproject/


    		
  

  

  

    
      68
    
    
      
      assert_no_tag :tag => 'a', :content => /Issue on project 2/


    		
  

  

  

    
      69
    
    
      
      # project column

      71
    
    
      
    end

  def test_index_with_short_filters


    		
  

  

  

    
      152
    
    
      
    to_test = {


    		
  

  

  

    
      153
    
    
      
      'status_id' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      154
    
    
      
        'o' => { :op => 'o', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      155
    
    
      
        'c' => { :op => 'c', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      156
    
    
      
        '7' => { :op => '=', :values => ['7'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      157
    
    
      
        '7|3|4' => { :op => '=', :values => ['7', '3', '4'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      158
    
    
      
        '=7' => { :op => '=', :values => ['7'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      159
    
    
      
        '!3' => { :op => '!', :values => ['3'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      160
    
    
      
        '!7|3|4' => { :op => '!', :values => ['7', '3', '4'] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      161
    
    
      
      'subject' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      162
    
    
      
        'This is a subject' => { :op => '=', :values => ['This is a subject'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      163
    
    
      
        'o' => { :op => '=', :values => ['o'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      164
    
    
      
        '~This is part of a subject' => { :op => '~', :values => ['This is part of a subject'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      165
    
    
      
        '!~This is part of a subject' => { :op => '!~', :values => ['This is part of a subject'] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      166
    
    
      
      'tracker_id' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      167
    
    
      
        '3' => { :op => '=', :values => ['3'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      168
    
    
      
        '=3' => { :op => '=', :values => ['3'] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      169
    
    
      
      'start_date' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      170
    
    
      
        '2011-10-12' => { :op => '=', :values => ['2011-10-12'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      171
    
    
      
        '=2011-10-12' => { :op => '=', :values => ['2011-10-12'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      172
    
    
      
        '>=2011-10-12' => { :op => '>=', :values => ['2011-10-12'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      173
    
    
      
        '<=2011-10-12' => { :op => '<=', :values => ['2011-10-12'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      174
    
    
      
        '><2011-10-01|2011-10-30' => { :op => '><', :values => ['2011-10-01', '2011-10-30'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      175
    
    
      
        '<t+2' => { :op => '<t+', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      176
    
    
      
        '>t+2' => { :op => '>t+', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      177
    
    
      
        't+2' => { :op => 't+', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      178
    
    
      
        't' => { :op => 't', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      179
    
    
      
        'w' => { :op => 'w', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      180
    
    
      
        '>t-2' => { :op => '>t-', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      181
    
    
      
        '<t-2' => { :op => '<t-', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      182
    
    
      
        't-2' => { :op => 't-', :values => ['2'] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      183
    
    
      
      'created_on' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      184
    
    
      
        '>=2011-10-12' => { :op => '>=', :values => ['2011-10-12'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      185
    
    
      
        '<t-2' => { :op => '<t-', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      186
    
    
      
        '>t-2' => { :op => '>t-', :values => ['2'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      187
    
    
      
        't-2' => { :op => 't-', :values => ['2'] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      188
    
    
      
      'cf_1' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      189
    
    
      
        'c' => { :op => '=', :values => ['c'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      190
    
    
      
        '!c' => { :op => '!', :values => ['c'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      191
    
    
      
        '!*' => { :op => '!*', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      192
    
    
      
        '*' => { :op => '*', :values => [''] }},


    		
  

  

  

    
      193
    
    
      
      'estimated_hours' => {


    		
  

  

  

    
      194
    
    
      
        '=13.4' => { :op => '=', :values => ['13.4'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      195
    
    
      
        '>=45' => { :op => '>=', :values => ['45'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      196
    
    
      
        '<=125' => { :op => '<=', :values => ['125'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      197
    
    
      
        '><10.5|20.5' => { :op => '><', :values => ['10.5', '20.5'] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      198
    
    
      
        '!*' => { :op => '!*', :values => [''] },


    		
  

  

  

    
      199
    
    
      
        '*' => { :op => '*', :values => [''] }}


    		
  

  

  

    
      200
    
    
      
    }


    		
  

  

  

    
      201
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      202
    
    
      
    default_filter = { 'status_id' => {:operator => 'o', :values => [''] }}


    		
  

  

  

    
      203
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      204
    
    
      
    to_test.each do |field, expression_and_expected|


    		
  

  

  

    
      205
    
    
      
      expression_and_expected.each do |filter_expression, expected|


    		
  

  

  

    
      206
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      207
    
    
      
        get :index, :set_filter => 1, field => filter_expression


    		
  

  

  

    
      208
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      209
    
    
      
        assert_response :success


    		
  

  

  

    
      210
    
    
      
        assert_template 'index'


    		
  

  

  

    
      211
    
    
      
        assert_not_nil assigns(:issues)


    		
  

  

  

    
      212
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      213
    
    
      
        query = assigns(:query)


    		
  

  

  

    
      214
    
    
      
        assert_not_nil query


    		
  

  

  

    
      215
    
    
      
        assert query.has_filter?(field)


    		
  

  

  

    
      216
    
    
      
        assert_equal(default_filter.merge({field => {:operator => expected[:op], :values => expected[:values]}}), query.filters)


    		
  

  

  

    
      217
    
    
      
      end


    		
  

  

  

    
      218
    
    
      
    end


    		
  

  

  

    
      219
    
    
      
  end

  def test_index_csv_big_5


    		
  

  

  

    
      378
    
    
      
    with_settings :default_language => "zh-TW" do


    		
  

  

  

    
      379
    
    
      
      str_utf8  = "\xe4\xb8\x80\xe6\x9c\x88"


    		
  

  

  

    
      380
    
    
      
      str_big5  = "\xa4@\xa4\xeb"


    		
  

  

  

    
      381
    
    
      
      if str_utf8.respond_to?(:force_encoding)


    		
  

  

  

    
      382
    
    
      
        str_utf8.force_encoding('UTF-8')


    		
  

  

  

    
      383
    
    
      
        str_big5.force_encoding('Big5')


    		
  

  

  

    
      384
    
    
      
      end


    		
  

  

  

    
      385
    
    
      
      issue = Issue.new(:project_id => 1, :tracker_id => 1, :author_id => 3,


    		
  

  

  

    
      386
    
    
      
                        :status_id => 1, :priority => IssuePriority.all.first,


    		
  

  

  

    
      387
    
    
      
                        :subject => str_utf8)


    		
  

  

  

    
      388
    
    
      
      assert issue.save

      390
    
    
      
      get :index, :project_id => 1, 


    		
  

  

  

    
      391
    
    
      
                  :f => ['subject'], 


    		
  

  

  

    
      392
    
    
      
                  :op => '=', :values => [str_utf8],


    		
  

  

  

    
      393
    
    
      
                  :format => 'csv'


    		
  

  

  

    
      394
    
    
      
      assert_equal 'text/csv', @response.content_type


    		
  

  

  

    
      395
    
    
      
      lines = @response.body.chomp.split("\n")


    		
  

  

  

    
      396
    
    
      
      s1 = "\xaa\xac\xbaA"


    		
  

  

  

    
      397
    
    
      
      if str_utf8.respond_to?(:force_encoding)


    		
  

  

  

    
      398
    
    
      
        s1.force_encoding('Big5')


    		
  

  

  

    
      399

  end

  def test_index_csv_cannot_convert_should_be_replaced_big_5


    		
  

  

  

    
      406
    
    
      
    with_settings :default_language => "zh-TW" do


    		
  

  

  

    
      407
    
    
      
      str_utf8  = "\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe5\x86\x85"


    		
  

  

  

    
      408
    
    
      
      if str_utf8.respond_to?(:force_encoding)


    		
  

  

  

    
      409
    
    
      
        str_utf8.force_encoding('UTF-8')


    		
  

  

  

    
      410
    
    
      
      end


    		
  

  

  

    
      411
    
    
      
      issue = Issue.new(:project_id => 1, :tracker_id => 1, :author_id => 3,


    		
  

  

  

    
      412
    
    
      
                        :status_id => 1, :priority => IssuePriority.all.first,


    		
  

  

  

    
      413

                  :f => ['subject'],

                  :op => '=', :values => [str_utf8],


    		
  

  

  

    
      419

      421

      422
    
    
      
      assert_equal 'text/csv', @response.content_type


    		
  

  

  

    
      423
    
    
      
      lines = @response.body.chomp.split("\n")


    		
  

  

  

    
      424
    
    
      
      s1 = "\xaa\xac\xbaA" # status


    		
  

  

  

    
      425
    
    
      
      if str_utf8.respond_to?(:force_encoding)

      430
    
    
      
      if s1.respond_to?(:force_encoding)


    		
  

  

  

    
      431
    
    
      
        s3 = "\xa5H?" # subject


    		
  

  

  

    
      432
    
    
      
        s3.force_encoding('Big5')


    		
  

  

  

    
      433
    
    
      
        assert_equal s3, s2


    		
  

  

  

    
      434
    
    
      
      elsif RUBY_PLATFORM == 'java'


    		
  

  

  

    
      435
    
    
      
        assert_equal "??", s2


    		
  

  

  

    
      436

  def test_index_csv_fr

  def test_post_create


    		
  

  

  

    
      1392
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      1393
    
    
      
    assert_difference 'Issue.count' do


    		
  

  

  

    
      1394
    
    
      
      post :create, :project_id => 1,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1395
    
    
      
                 :issue => {:tracker_id => 3,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1396
    
    
      
                            :status_id => 2,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1397
    
    
      
                            :subject => 'This is the test_new issue',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1398
    
    
      
                            :description => 'This is the description',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1399
    
    
      
                            :priority_id => 5,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1400
    
    
      
                            :start_date => '2010-11-07',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1401
    
    
      
                            :estimated_hours => '',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1402
    
    
      
                            :custom_field_values => {'2' => 'Value for field 2'}}


    		
  

  

  

    
      1403
    
    
      
    end


    		
  

  

  

    
      1404
    
    
      
    assert_redirected_to :controller => 'issues', :action => 'show', :id => Issue.last.id


    		
  

  

  

    
      1405
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      1406
    
    
      
    issue = Issue.find_by_subject('This is the test_new issue')


    		
  

  

  

    
      1407
    
    
      
    assert_not_nil issue


    		
  

  

  

    
      1408
    
    
      
    assert_equal 2, issue.author_id


    		
  

  

  

    
      1409
    
    
      
    assert_equal 3, issue.tracker_id


    		
  

  

  

    
      1410
    
    
      
    assert_equal 2, issue.status_id


    		
  

  

  

    
      1411
    
    
      
    assert_equal Date.parse('2010-11-07'), issue.start_date


    		
  

  

  

    
      1412
    
    
      
    assert_nil issue.estimated_hours


    		
  

  

  

    
      1413
    
    
      
    v = issue.custom_values.find(:first, :conditions => {:custom_field_id => 2})


    		
  

  

  

    
      1414
    
    
      
    assert_not_nil v


    		
  

  

  

    
      1415
    
    
      
    assert_equal 'Value for field 2', v.value


    		
  

  

  

    
      1416
    
    
      
  end

  def test_post_create_with_watchers


    		
  

  

  

    
      1582
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      1583
    
    
      
    ActionMailer::Base.deliveries.clear


    		
  

  

  

    
      1584
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      1585
    
    
      
    assert_difference 'Watcher.count', 2 do


    		
  

  

  

    
      1586
    
    
      
      post :create, :project_id => 1,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1587
    
    
      
                 :issue => {:tracker_id => 1,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1588
    
    
      
                            :subject => 'This is a new issue with watchers',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1589
    
    
      
                            :description => 'This is the description',


    		
  

  

  

    
      1590
    
    
      
                            :priority_id => 5,


    		
  

  

  

    
      1591
    
    
      
                            :watcher_user_ids => ['2', '3']}


    		
  

  

  

    
      1592
    
    
      
    end


    		
  

  

  

    
      1593
    
    
      
    issue = Issue.find_by_subject('This is a new issue with watchers')


    		
  

  

  

    
      1594
    
    
      
    assert_not_nil issue


    		
  

  

  

    
      1595

      1597

      1598

      1600

      1601

      1602
    
    
      
    assert_not_nil mail


    		
  

  

  

    
      1603

      1604
    
    
      
  end

  def test_post_create_private_with_set_own_issues_private_permission

  def test_new_as_copy

  def test_put_update_without_custom_fields_param


    		
  

  

  

    
      2238
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      2239
    
    
      
    ActionMailer::Base.deliveries.clear


    		
  

  

  

    
      2240
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2241
    
    
      
    issue = Issue.find(1)


    		
  

  

  

    
      2242
    
    
      
    assert_equal '125', issue.custom_value_for(2).value


    		
  

  

  

    
      2243
    
    
      
    old_subject = issue.subject


    		
  

  

  

    
      2244
    
    
      
    new_subject = 'Subject modified by IssuesControllerTest#test_post_edit'


    		
  

  

  

    
      2245
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2246
    
    
      
    assert_difference('Journal.count') do


    		
  

  

  

    
      2247
    
    
      
      assert_difference('JournalDetail.count', 2) do


    		
  

  

  

    
      2248
    
    
      
        put :update, :id => 1, :issue => {:subject => new_subject,


    		
  

  

  

    
      2249
    
    
      
                                         :priority_id => '6',


    		
  

  

  

    
      2250
    
    
      
                                         :category_id => '1' # no change


    		
  

  

  

    
      2251
    
    
      
                                        }


    		
  

  

  

    
      2252
    
    
      
      end


    		
  

  

  

    
      2253
    
    
      
    end


    		
  

  

  

    
      2254
    
    
      
    assert_redirected_to :action => 'show', :id => '1'


    		
  

  

  

    
      2255
    
    
      
    issue.reload


    		
  

  

  

    
      2256
    
    
      
    assert_equal new_subject, issue.subject


    		
  

  

  

    
      2257
    
    
      
    # Make sure custom fields were not cleared


    		
  

  

  

    
      2258
    
    
      
    assert_equal '125', issue.custom_value_for(2).value


    		
  

  

  

    
      2259
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2260
    
    
      
    mail = ActionMailer::Base.deliveries.last


    		
  

  

  

    
      2261
    
    
      
    assert_not_nil mail


    		
  

  

  

    
      2262
    
    
      
    assert mail.subject.starts_with?("[#{issue.project.name} - #{issue.tracker.name} ##{issue.id}]")


    		
  

  

  

    
      2263
    
    
      
    assert_mail_body_match "Subject changed from #{old_subject} to #{new_subject}", mail


    		
  

  

  

    
      2264
    
    
      
  end

  def test_put_update_with_multi_custom_field_change

  def test_bulk_update


    		
  

  

  

    
      2790
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      2791
    
    
      
    # update issues priority


    		
  

  

  

    
      2792
    
    
      
    post :bulk_update, :ids => [1, 2], :notes => 'Bulk editing',


    		
  

  

  

    
      2793
    
    
      
                                     :issue => {:priority_id => 7,


    		
  

  

  

    
      2794
    
    
      
                                                :assigned_to_id => '',


    		
  

  

  

    
      2795
    
    
      
                                                :custom_field_values => {'2' => ''}}


    		
  

  

  

    
      2796
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2797
    
    
      
    assert_response 302


    		
  

  

  

    
      2798
    
    
      
    # check that the issues were updated


    		
  

  

  

    
      2799
    
    
      
    assert_equal [7, 7], Issue.find_all_by_id([1, 2]).collect {|i| i.priority.id}


    		
  

  

  

    
      2800
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2801
    
    
      
    issue = Issue.find(1)


    		
  

  

  

    
      2802
    
    
      
    journal = issue.journals.find(:first, :order => 'created_on DESC')


    		
  

  

  

    
      2803
    
    
      
    assert_equal '125', issue.custom_value_for(2).value


    		
  

  

  

    
      2804
    
    
      
    assert_equal 'Bulk editing', journal.notes


    		
  

  

  

    
      2805
    
    
      
    assert_equal 1, journal.details.size


    		
  

  

  

    
      2806
    
    
      
  end

  def test_bulk_update_on_different_projects


    		
  

  

  

    
      2825
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      2826
    
    
      
    # update issues priority


    		
  

  

  

    
      2827

      2828

      2829

      2833

      2834
    
    
      
    assert_equal [7, 7, 7], Issue.find([1,2,6]).map(&:priority_id)


    		
  

  

  

    
      2835
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      2836

  def test_destroy_parent_and_child_issues


    		
  

  

  

    
      3218
    
    
      
    parent = Issue.create!(:project_id => 1, :author_id => 1, :tracker_id => 1, :subject => 'Parent Issue')


    		
  

  

  

    
      3219
    
    
      
    child = Issue.create!(:project_id => 1, :author_id => 1, :tracker_id => 1, :subject => 'Child Issue', :parent_issue_id => parent.id)


    		
  

  

  

    
      3220
    
    
      
    assert child.is_descendant_of?(parent.reload)


    		
  

  

  

    
      3221
    
    
      

    		
  

  

  

    
      3222
    
    
      
    @request.session[:user_id] = 2


    		
  

  

  

    
      3223
    
    
      
    assert_difference 'Issue.count', -2 do


    		
  

  

  

    
      3224
    
    
      
      delete :destroy, :ids => [parent.id, child.id], :todo => 'destroy'


    		
  

  

  

    
      3225
    
    
      
    end


    		
  

  

  

    
      3226
    
    
      
    assert_response 302


    		
  

  

  

    
      3227
    
    
      
  end
